================================================================================
File: README.md
================================================================================

# Tower — Incremental Physics Builder

Build towering structures in a living physics world. Place blocks, manage resources, research upgrades, and push your tower to the sky — until the welds snap.

---

## Overview

Tower is an **incremental/idle physics builder** built with vanilla HTML5 Canvas and [Matter.js](https://brm.io/matter-js/). Every block has real mass, every weld carries real stress, and every collapse is simulated in real time.

**Core loop:**

1. **Place blocks** to grow your tower skyward.
2. **Earn passive income** that scales with tower height.
3. **Buy upgrades** to reduce stress, automate building, and unlock new materials.
4. **Prestige** to reset the visible tower in exchange for permanent income multipliers.
5. **Unlock achievements** as you hit milestones — then try to reach even higher.

---

## Quick Start

No build step, no bundler, no install. Open in any modern browser:

```bash
cd tower
python3 -m http.server 8080
# or
npx serve .
```

Then open `http://localhost:8080` in your browser.

> **Note**: Matter.js is loaded from a CDN (`matter-js 0.20.0`). An internet connection is required on first load.

---

## Controls

| Input | Action |
|---|---|
| **Left-click** on valid position | Place a block |
| **Right-click / Middle-click + drag** | Pan camera |
| **Scroll wheel** | Zoom in / out (cursor stays fixed) |
| **G** | Toggle grid snap |
| **R** | Cycle material (concrete → steel → reinforced) |

Blocks snap to a 10‑unit grid by default. Toggle it off with **G** for free placement.

---

## Architecture (~6,000 lines)

The game is organised as **13 ES6 modules** coordinated by a strict `GameLoop` with a fixed per-frame execution order:

```
Phase  1: InputManager      — mouse, keyboard, touch, ghost preview, camera
Phase  2: EconomyManager    — passive income, upgrade purchase, resource validation
Phase  3: StatTracker       — cumulative metrics, height/prestige change detection
Phase  4: AchievementManager — data-driven achievement checking
Phase  5: AutomationManager — auto-builder drone
Phase  6: PhysicsEngine     — Matter.js step, body/constraint lifecycle, wind
Phase  7: EventManager      — random wind gusts, micro-impulses
Phase  8: StressSolver      — read constraint forces, break overstressed welds
Phase  9: RenderManager     — Canvas 2D: sky, parallax, blocks, stress heatmap, floating text
Phase 10: UIManager         — DOM HUD: resources, upgrades, prestige, toaster
Phase 11: SaveManager       — localStorage persistence (autosave + on-unload)
          AudioManager      — Web Audio API procedural sounds (no asset files)
          PrestigeSystem    — reset logic, reward computation, multiplier recalculation
          GameLoop          — RAF orchestrator, dt capping, phase ordering
```

### Single Source of Truth

All mutable game data lives in a single serialisable `GameState` object:

```
gameState {
  resources: { money, steel, research }
  upgrades:  { "reinforced_steel": { level: 5 }, ... }
  tower:     { blocks: [{id, x, y, width, height, materialId, stress, ...}],
               currentHeight, maxHeight }
  camera:    { x, y, zoom, targetBlockId }
  placement: { active, worldX, worldY, valid, snapEnabled, snapSize, materialId }
  achievements: { unlocked: ["first_brick", ...] }
  prestige:  { currency, multipliers: { money, steel }, resetCount }
  settings:  { quality, sound, autosaveInterval, musicEnabled }
  stats:     { totalBlocksPlaced, totalCollapses, playTime,
               totalMoneyEarned, totalSteelEarned, totalResearchEarned,
               totalUpgradesPurchased, upgradesMaxed }
}
```

Every module receives the same `GameState` reference at init and reads/writes through it. No module owns private copies of global state.

---

## Physics Model

Matter.js handles all rigid-body dynamics:

- **Materials**: concrete (density 0.0025), steel (0.004), reinforced (0.005)
- **Welds**: each new block is constrained to the blocks directly below it via `Matter.Constraint` with material‑dependent stiffness, damping, and `maxForce`
- **Stress**: after every physics step, the `StressSolver` reads `constraint.reaction` on every weld. If `|reaction| > maxForce`, the weld snaps — the constraint is removed and the blocks separate
- **Wind**: altitude‑scaled horizontal force: `force(y) = baseForce × (1 + |y| / 300)`. Higher blocks catch more wind (boundary‑layer approximation)
- **Culling**: blocks falling below `y = 5000` are removed from both the physics world and GameState

---

## Upgrade System

Upgrades are defined as data in `js/data/upgrades.json` and loaded synchronously by the `EconomyManager`. The schema:

```json
{
  "id": "reinforced_steel",
  "name": "Reinforced Steel",
  "tier": 1,
  "maxLevel": 50,
  "baseCost": { "money": 100, "steel": 50 },
  "costMultiplier": 1.15,
  "effectType": "stress_reduction",
  "baseValue": 0.03,
  "valuePerLevel": 0.03
}
```

**Cost formula**: `cost(r) = baseCost[r] × costMultiplier ^ level`

**Effect query**: Any module calls `economy.getEffectValue('stress_reduction')` which sums `baseValue + level × valuePerLevel` across all upgrades of that type.

### Available Upgrades

| Upgrade | Tier | Effect | Max Level |
|---|---|---|---|
| Reinforced Steel | 1 | −3 % stress per level | 50 |
| Auto-Builder Drone | 1 | −0.15 s auto‑build interval per level | 20 |
| Wind Dampener | 2 | −6 % wind force per level | 15 |
| Advanced Alloys | 2 | +10 % block health per level | 30 |
| Prestige Amplifier | 3 | +5 % prestige token yield per level | 10 |

---

## Prestige Cycle

Once `maxHeight ≥ 500`, the prestige button becomes active.

**Reward formula**:
```
base     = floor(sqrt(maxHeight × 0.5))
amplifier = 1 + getEffectValue('prestige_amplifier')
tokens   = floor(base × amplifier)

Examples:
  height  500 →  15 tokens
  height 2000 →  31 tokens
  height 8000 →  63 tokens
```

**Each prestige token** adds +10 % to money and steel income:
```
multiplier = 1 + tokens × 0.10
```

**Reset preserves**: prestige tokens, multipliers, upgrades, settings, collapse count, play time.

---

## Achievement System

20 data‑driven achievements with four condition types:

| Type | Condition |
|---|---|
| `stat_ge` | `stats[stat] >= threshold` |
| `max_height_ge` | `tower.maxHeight >= threshold` |
| `prestige_count` | `prestige.resetCount >= threshold` |
| `upgrade_level` | `upgrades[id].level >= threshold` |

Achievements are checked reactively — the `StatTracker` emits events on stat changes, the `AchievementManager` evaluates locked achievements, and the `UIManager` shows a slide‑in toast notification with a CSS animation.

Unlocked achievements persist in `GameState.achievements.unlocked` and survive save/load.

---

## Audio

All sounds are **procedurally generated** via the Web Audio API — no audio files, no CORS issues:

| Trigger | Sound |
|---|---|
| Block placed | 80–120 Hz sine, 120 ms decay |
| UI click | 800–1200 Hz sine, 40 ms decay |
| Collapse | Sawtooth sweep + noise burst, 500 ms |
| Achievement | C5→E5→G5 ascending arpeggio |
| Ambience | A1 (55 Hz) + A0 (27.5 Hz) drone, looped |

The `AudioContext` is created on the first user gesture (click / keydown) per browser autoplay policy.

---

## Rendering (Three.js WebGL)

The `RenderManager` uses a Three.js OrthographicCamera for exact 1:1 pixel mapping with Matter.js coordinates. The Y axis is flipped (Matter.js Y-down → Three.js Y-up) so the tower grows upward.

Rendering order (bottom to top):

1. **Sky gradient** — deep‑space black to horizon blue, shifts with camera Y
2. **Mountains** — two parallax layers (depth 0.5 / 0.7)
3. **Clouds** — 30 ellipses at depth 0.15–0.35
4. **Ground line** + subtle grid
5. **Blocks** — coloured by material, frustum‑culled, 3‑px bevel, stress overlay tint
6. **Stress heatmap** — constraint lines coloured green→yellow→red
7. **Snap particles** — white circles that grow and fade on weld break
8. **Ghost preview** — translucent green (valid) or red (invalid)
9. **Floating text** — "+$15", "-10" popups that float and fade
10. **Crosshair** — centre‑screen indicator

---

## Save System

Saves are written to `localStorage` under the key `tower_save`:

- **Autosave** every 30 seconds
- **On‑unload save** when the page closes
- **Manual wipe** button (double‑click confirmation) in the bottom‑right corner

The save payload includes the full `GameState` plus module‑level data (PhysicsEngine body positions/velocities, AutomationManager counters) so the game resumes identically. Corrupt or schema‑mismatched saves are silently discarded.

---

## Project Structure

```
tower/
├── index.html              ← Entry point + CSS layout + HUD
├── README.md
└── js/
    ├── main.js             ← Bootstrap, module wiring, cross-module event chains
    ├── state.js            ← GameState typedef, factory, clone, validation
    ├── constants.js        ← All tunable numbers
    ├── math.js             ← Pure scaling formulas
    ├── core/
    │   ├── GameLoop.js     ← RAF orchestrator, dt capping, phase ordering
    │   ├── InputManager.js ← Pointer/keyboard capture, ghost preview, camera
    │   ├── EconomyManager.js ← Income, upgrades, resource validation
    │   ├── StatTracker.js  ← Cumulative metric monitor + event emitter
    │   ├── AchievementManager.js ← Data-driven achievement checker
    │   ├── AutomationManager.js  ← Auto-builder drone
    │   ├── PhysicsEngine.js ← Matter.js wrapper, welds, wind, serialization
    │   ├── EventManager.js ← Random wind gusts, micro-impulses
    │   ├── StressSolver.js ← Constraint-force stress reader, weld breaker
    │   ├── RenderManager.js ← Canvas 2D: camera, parallax, blocks, stress, FX
    │   ├── UIManager.js    ← DOM HUD: resources, upgrades, prestige, toaster
    │   ├── SaveManager.js  ← localStorage persistence + validation
    │   ├── AudioManager.js ← Web Audio API procedural sounds
    │   └── PrestigeSystem.js ← Reset + reward + multiplier recalculation
    └── data/
        ├── upgrades.json       ← Upgrade definitions (5 upgrades)
        └── achievements.json   ← Achievement definitions (20 achievements)
```

---

## Development

All modules are standard ES modules — no transpiler, no bundler. Loaded directly in the browser via `<script type="module">`.

To add a new upgrade:
1. Add its definition to `js/data/upgrades.json` and the `UPGRADE_DEFS` array in `EconomyManager.js`
2. Use `economy.getEffectValue('your_effect_type')` in the consuming module

To add a new achievement:
1. Add its definition to `js/data/achievements.json` and the `ACHIEVEMENT_DEFS` array in `AchievementManager.js`
2. Condition types: `stat_ge`, `max_height_ge`, `prestige_count`, `upgrade_level`

---

## Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Physics | [Matter.js](https://brm.io/matter-js/) 0.20.0 |
| Rendering | Three.js WebGL (r160) |
| UI | Vanilla DOM (CSS Grid/Flexbox) |
| Audio | Web Audio API (procedural synthesis) |
| Persistence | localStorage |
| Modules | ES6 (`import` / `export`) |
| Dependencies | None — Matter.js loaded from CDN |

---

*Built in 7 phases across ~6,000 lines of vanilla JavaScript.*

---

## Audit & Known Issues

The codebase was subjected to a full systems audit covering state integrity, physics memory management, math safety, and rendering performance. **12 issues** were identified and fixed.

### Critical Fixes Applied

| # | Issue | Fix |
|---|-------|-----|
| 1 | `EventManager.js`: `const Matter = window.Matter;` was inside a JSDoc `/** */` block — micro-impulse events crashed with `ReferenceError` | Moved the declaration outside the comment block |
| 2 | `main.js`: StressSolver patch removed blocks from GameState but never called `physics.destroyBlock()` — orphan Matter bodies leaked on every collapse | Added `physics.destroyBlock(blockId)` before GameState removal |
| 3 | `PhysicsEngine.deserialize()`: Created a new ground body each save-load without removing the old one — accumulating duplicate grounds | Added `Composite.remove()` of old ground before rebuilding |
| 4 | `main.js` + `GameLoop.js`: SaveManager was never registered in the phase list — autosave timer searched for a phase named `'SaveManager'` that didn't exist | Added `loop.register({name:'SaveManager', ...})` to the phase list |

### High / Medium Fixes

| # | Issue | Fix |
|---|-------|-----|
| 5 | `main.js`: `input._placeBlock` was completely replaced (duplicating all placement logic) instead of wrapping the original | Changed to call `origPlaceBlock()` then inject hooks |
| 6 | `main.js`: Used `ui._short()` — a private UIManager method, breaking encapsulation | Moved `formatNumber`/`formatShort` to `math.js` as exported functions, imported by both UIManager and main.js |
| 7 | `main.js`: Same replacement pattern for `automation._autoPlaceBlock` | Changed to wrapper pattern |
| 8 | `EconomyManager.js`: Height factor was additive in income formula (income started at 2× at height 0) | Changed to multiplicative: `base × prestige × heightFactor × (1 + upgradeBonus)` |
| 9 | `PhysicsEngine._cullFallenBlocks()`: Incremented `totalCollapses` for harmless debris removal | Removed the increment (collapses are tracked by StressSolver only) |
| 10 | `UIManager._eng(n)`: Returned `"Infinityundefined"` for NaN inputs | Delegated to `formatNumber()` from `math.js` which has a `!Number.isFinite` guard |
| 11 | `math.js costExponential()`: Overflows to `Infinity` at extreme upgrade levels, propagating through cost checks | Added `!Number.isFinite(result)` guard that returns `MAX_SAFE_INTEGER` |
| 12 | `AchievementManager.js`: "Self-Aware" achievement referenced `state.stats.otherAchievements` which doesn't exist | Added `other_achievements` condition type that counts actually-unlocked achievements |

### Architecture Invariants Preserved

- **Single source of truth**: Every module receives the same `GameState` reference; no module creates isolated local copies of global state
- **Strict phase ordering**: The 11-phase GameLoop order is enforced and cannot be mutated at runtime
- **Deterministic math**: All scaling formulas are pure functions — no side effects, no global state dependencies
- **Safe persistence**: Save/load errors are caught silently; corrupt data is discarded, never thrown
- **Cross-module decoupling**: Modules communicate through GameState mutation and the StatTracker event bus, never by direct references to sibling internals

File: deploy-wrapper.js
================================================================================

// Monkey-patch Node.js DNS to resolve api.vercel.com via our custom resolver
const dns = require('dns');
const net = require('net');

const OVERRIDES = {
  'api.vercel.com': '76.76.21.112',
  'vercel.com': '64.239.123.65',
};

const originalLookup = dns.lookup;
dns.lookup = function(hostname, options, callback) {
  if (typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = {};
  }
  if (OVERRIDES[hostname]) {
    const ip = OVERRIDES[hostname];
    const family = net.isIPv4(ip) ? 4 : 6;
    if (callback) {
      callback(null, ip, family);
    }
    return;
  }
  originalLookup.call(dns, hostname, options, callback);
};

const originalResolve4 = dns.resolve4;
dns.resolve4 = function(hostname, options, callback) {
  if (typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = {};
  }
  if (OVERRIDES[hostname]) {
    if (callback) callback(null, [OVERRIDES[hostname]]);
    return;
  }
  originalResolve4.call(dns, hostname, options, callback);
};

const originalResolve = dns.resolve;
dns.resolve = function(hostname, rrtype, options, callback) {
  if (typeof options === 'function') {
    callback = options;
    options = {};
  }
  if (OVERRIDES[hostname] && (!rrtype || rrtype === 'A' || rrtype === 'ANY')) {
    if (callback) callback(null, [OVERRIDES[hostname]]);
    return;
  }
  originalResolve.call(dns, hostname, rrtype, options, callback);
};

// Now run the vercel deploy command
const { spawn } = require('child_process');
const args = ['deploy', '--prod', '--yes', ...process.argv.slice(2)];
const child = spawn('/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/vercel', args, {
  cwd: '/data/data/com.termux/files/home/dev/codex/games/tower',
  stdio: 'inherit',
  env: { ...process.env, NODE_OPTIONS: '' }
});

child.on('exit', (code) => {
  process.exit(code);
});

<!-- ── Overview ──────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="overview">
<h2>Overview</h2>
<p>Tower is an <strong>incremental / idle physics builder</strong> built with vanilla HTML5 Canvas and <a href="https://brm.io/matter-js/" target="_blank">Matter.js</a>. Every block has real mass, every weld carries real stress, and every collapse is simulated in real time.</p>

<h3>Core Loop</h3>
<ol>
  <li><strong>Place blocks</strong> to grow your tower skyward.</li>
  <li><strong>Earn passive income</strong> that scales with tower height.</li>
  <li><strong>Buy upgrades</strong> to reduce stress, automate building, and unlock new materials.</li>
  <li><strong>Prestige</strong> to reset the visible tower in exchange for permanent income multipliers.</li>
  <li><strong>Unlock achievements</strong> as you hit milestones — then reach even higher.</li>
</ol>
</section>

<!-- ── Quick Start ───────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="quick-start">
<h2>Quick Start</h2>
<p>No build step, no bundler, no install. Open in any modern browser:</p>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">bash</span>cd tower
python3 -m http.server 8080
# or
npx serve .</pre>
<p>Then open <a href="http://localhost:8080" target="_blank">http://localhost:8080</a>.</p>

<div class="callout info">
  <strong>Note:</strong> Matter.js is loaded from a CDN (<code>matter-js 0.20.0</code>). An internet connection is required on first load.
</div>
</section>

<!-- ── Controls ──────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="controls">
<h2>Controls</h2>
<table>
  <tr><th>Input</th><th>Action</th></tr>
  <tr><td><kbd>Left-click</kbd> on valid position</td><td>Place a block</td></tr>
  <tr><td><kbd>Right-click</kbd> / <kbd>Middle-click</kbd> + drag</td><td>Pan camera</td></tr>
  <tr><td><kbd>Scroll wheel</kbd></td><td>Zoom in / out (cursor stays fixed)</td></tr>
  <tr><td><kbd>G</kbd></td><td>Toggle grid snap</td></tr>
  <tr><td><kbd>R</kbd></td><td>Cycle material (concrete → steel → reinforced)</td></tr>
</table>
<p>Blocks snap to a 10‑unit grid by default. Toggle it off with <kbd>G</kbd> for free placement.</p>
</section>

<!-- ── Architecture ──────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="modules">
<h2>Module Architecture</h2>
<p>The game is organised as <strong>13 ES6 modules</strong> coordinated by a strict <code>GameLoop</code> with a fixed per-frame execution order. Each module follows the same lifecycle: <code>init(state)</code>, <code>update(dt)</code>, <code>serialize()</code>, <code>deserialize(data, state)</code>.</p>

<div class="phase-list">
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">1</span><span class="phase-name">InputManager</span><span class="phase-desc">Mouse / keyboard / touch capture, ghost preview, camera pan &amp; zoom</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">2</span><span class="phase-name">EconomyManager</span><span class="phase-desc">Passive income, upgrade purchase, resource validation</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">3</span><span class="phase-name">StatTracker</span><span class="phase-desc">Cumulative metrics, height / prestige change detection</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">4</span><span class="phase-name">AchievementManager</span><span class="phase-desc">Data-driven achievement checking</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">5</span><span class="phase-name">AutomationManager</span><span class="phase-desc">Auto-builder drone</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">6</span><span class="phase-name">PhysicsEngine</span><span class="phase-desc">Matter.js step, body / constraint lifecycle, wind</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">7</span><span class="phase-name">EventManager</span><span class="phase-desc">Random wind gusts, micro-impulses</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">8</span><span class="phase-name">StressSolver</span><span class="phase-desc">Read constraint forces, break overstressed welds</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">9</span><span class="phase-name">RenderManager</span><span class="phase-desc">Canvas 2D: sky, parallax, blocks, stress heatmap, floating text</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">10</span><span class="phase-name">UIManager</span><span class="phase-desc">DOM HUD: resources, upgrades, prestige panel, achievement toaster</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row"><span class="phase-num">11</span><span class="phase-name">SaveManager</span><span class="phase-desc">localStorage persistence (autosave + on-unload)</span></div>
</div>
<div class="phase-list">
  <div class="phase-row" style="padding-left:40px"><span class="phase-name" style="width:auto">AudioManager</span><span class="phase-desc">Web Audio API procedural sounds (no asset files required)</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row" style="padding-left:40px"><span class="phase-name" style="width:auto">PrestigeSystem</span><span class="phase-desc">Reset logic, reward computation, multiplier recalculation</span></div>
  <div class="phase-row" style="padding-left:40px"><span class="phase-name" style="width:auto">GameLoop</span><span class="phase-desc">RAF orchestrator, dt capping, phase ordering</span></div>
</div>
</section>

<!-- ── Game Loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="game-loop">
<h2>Game Loop Execution Order</h2>
<p>The <code>GameLoop</code> uses <code>requestAnimationFrame</code> with a hard cap of 50 ms per frame to prevent physics spiral-of-death after tab-away. The execution order within each tick is:</p>

<pre><span class="lang-tag">fixed order</span> 1. Input           ← ghost calc, placement, camera
 2. Economy         ← passive income, offline catch-up
 3. Stats           ← detect maxHeight / prestige changes
 4. Achievements    ← check locked achievements
 5. Automation      ← AI block placement
 6. Physics         ← Matter.js step, constraint.reaction set
 7. Events          ← wind gusts, micro-impulses
 8. Stress          ← read constraint forces, break welds
 9. Render          ← Canvas drawing (sky → blocks → FX)
10. UI              ← DOM HUD (throttled to 100 ms)
11. Autosave        ← interval-based (every 30 s)</pre>

<p>The critical ordering is <strong>Physics → Events → Stress</strong>: wind is applied AFTER the physics step but BEFORE the stress check, so wind loads are baked into the constraint reaction vectors when the solver evaluates them.</p>
</section>

<!-- ── GameState ─────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="state">
<h2>Single Source of Truth</h2>
<p>All mutable game data lives in one serialisable <code>GameState</code> object. Every module receives the same reference at init and reads / writes through it. No module owns private copies of global state.</p>

<details>
<summary>📄 <code>GameState</code> structure (click to expand)</summary>
<div class="detail-body">
<pre><span class="lang-tag">js</span>gameState {
  resources: { money, steel, research },
  upgrades:  { "reinforced_steel": { level: 5 }, ... },
  tower:     { blocks: [{ id, x, y, width, height, 
                           materialId, stress, health }],
               currentHeight, maxHeight },
  camera:    { x, y, zoom, targetBlockId },
  placement: { active, worldX, worldY, valid, snapEnabled, 
               snapSize, materialId },
  achievements: { unlocked: ["first_brick", ...] },
  prestige:  { currency, multipliers: { money, steel }, resetCount },
  settings:  { quality, sound, autosaveInterval, musicEnabled },
  stats:     { totalBlocksPlaced, totalCollapses, playTime,
               totalMoneyEarned, totalSteelEarned,
               totalResearchEarned, totalUpgradesPurchased,
               upgradesMaxed }
}</pre>
</div>
</details>
</section>

<!-- ── Physics ───────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="physics">
<h2>Physics Model</h2>
<p>Matter.js handles all rigid-body dynamics with custom weld constraints that simulate structural joints.</p>

<h3>Materials</h3>
<table>
  <tr><th>ID</th><th>Name</th><th>Density</th><th>Friction</th><th>Weld Stiffness</th><th>Weld Max Force</th></tr>
  <tr><td>0</td><td>Concrete</td><td>0.0025</td><td>0.8</td><td>0.65</td><td>80</td></tr>
  <tr><td>1</td><td>Steel</td><td>0.004</td><td>0.6</td><td>0.85</td><td>200</td></tr>
  <tr><td>2</td><td>Reinforced</td><td>0.005</td><td>0.7</td><td>0.93</td><td>400</td></tr>
</table>

<h3>Welds</h3>
<p>When a block is placed, the <code>PhysicsEngine</code> finds any blocks directly below it (within 6 units vertically, with horizontal overlap) and creates a <code>Matter.Constraint</code> with the material's <code>weldStiffness</code> and <code>weldMaxForce</code>.</p>

<h3>Stress &amp; Failure</h3>
<p>After every physics step, the <code>StressSolver</code> reads <code>constraint.reaction</code> — the instantaneous force vector the constraint is applying to keep the bodies together. If <code>|reaction| &gt; maxForce</code>, the weld snaps (the constraint is removed from the world). The block becomes loose and falls.</p>

<p>Block stress (displayed in the UI) is the average constraint force across all welds on that block, normalised so 1.0 = at the breaking point.</p>

<h3>Wind</h3>
<p>Altitude-scaled horizontal force applied each frame during a wind event:</p>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">math</span>force(y) = baseForce × (1 + |y| / heightScale)</pre>
<p>This models the atmospheric boundary layer — wind speed increases with height because surface friction diminishes.</p>

<h3>Collision Culling</h3>
<p>Blocks that fall below <code>y = 5000</code> are removed from both the Matter world and GameState to prevent orphan bodies from consuming CPU cycles.</p>
</section>

<!-- ── Upgrades ──────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="upgrades">
<h2>Upgrade System</h2>
<p>Upgrades are defined as data in <code>js/data/upgrades.json</code> and loaded synchronously by the <code>EconomyManager</code>.</p>

<h3>Schema</h3>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">json</span>{
  "id": "reinforced_steel",
  "name": "Reinforced Steel",
  "tier": 1,
  "maxLevel": 50,
  "baseCost": { "money": 100, "steel": 50 },
  "costMultiplier": 1.15,
  "effectType": "stress_reduction",
  "baseValue": 0.03,
  "valuePerLevel": 0.03
}</pre>

<h3>Cost Formula</h3>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">math</span>cost(resource) = baseCost[resource] × costMultiplier ^ level</pre>

<h3>Effect Query</h3>
<p>Any module calls <code>economy.getEffectValue('stress_reduction')</code> which sums <code>baseValue + level × valuePerLevel</code> across all upgrades of that type.</p>

<h3>Available Upgrades</h3>
<table>
  <tr><th>Upgrade</th><th>Tier</th><th>Effect</th><th>Max Level</th></tr>
  <tr><td>Reinforced Steel</td><td>1</td><td>−3 % stress per level</td><td>50</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Auto-Builder Drone</td><td>1</td><td>−0.15 s auto-build interval per level</td><td>20</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Wind Dampener</td><td>2</td><td>−6 % wind force per level</td><td>15</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Advanced Alloys</td><td>2</td><td>+10 % block health per level</td><td>30</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Prestige Amplifier</td><td>3</td><td>+5 % prestige token yield per level</td><td>10</td></tr>
</table>
</section>

<!-- ── Prestige ──────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="prestige">
<h2>Prestige Cycle</h2>
<p>Once <code>maxHeight ≥ 500</code>, the prestige button in the side panel becomes active.</p>

<h3>Reward Formula</h3>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">math</span>base     = ⌊√(maxHeight × 0.5)⌋
amplifier = 1 + getEffectValue('prestige_amplifier')
tokens    = ⌊base × amplifier⌋

Examples:
  height   500 →  15 tokens
  height  2000 →  31 tokens
  height  8000 →  63 tokens</pre>

<h3>Income Multiplier</h3>
<p>Each held prestige token adds +10 % to money and steel income:</p>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">math</span>multiplier = 1 + tokens × 0.10</pre>

<h3>Reset Preserves</h3>
<p>Prestige tokens, multipliers, upgrade levels, settings, collapse count, and play time survive the reset. Tower blocks, resources, and camera position are wiped to a fresh state.</p>
</section>

<!-- ── Achievements ──────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="achievements">
<h2>Achievement System</h2>
<p>20 data-driven achievements with four condition types, checked reactively via the <code>StatTracker</code> → <code>AchievementManager</code> event chain.</p>

<table>
  <tr><th>Condition Type</th><th>Example</th></tr>
  <tr><td><code>stat_ge</code></td><td><code>stats.totalBlocksPlaced >= 1000</code></td></tr>
  <tr><td><code>max_height_ge</code></td><td><code>tower.maxHeight >= 500</code></td></tr>
  <tr><td><code>prestige_count</code></td><td><code>prestige.resetCount >= 5</code></td></tr>
  <tr><td><code>upgrade_level</code></td><td><code>upgrades.auto_builder.level >= 20</code></td></tr>
</table>

<details>
<summary>🏆 Full achievement list (click to expand)</summary>
<div class="detail-body">
<table>
  <tr><th>Icon</th><th>Name</th><th>Condition</th></tr>

  <tr><td>🔨</td><td>Apprentice Builder</td><td>10 blocks placed</td></tr>

</section>

<!-- ── Audio ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="audio">
<h2>Audio Engine</h2>
<p>All sounds are <strong>procedurally generated</strong> via the Web Audio API — no audio files, no CORS issues, no preloading.</p>

<table>
  <tr><th>Trigger</th><th>Sound Design</th></tr>
  <tr><td>Block placed</td><td>80–120 Hz sine, 120 ms decay</td></tr>
  <tr><td>UI click</td><td>800–1200 Hz sine, 40 ms decay</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Collapse</td><td>Sawtooth sweep 60→20 Hz + white noise burst, 500 ms</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Achievement</td><td>C5→E5→G5 ascending arpeggio</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Ambience</td><td>A1 (55 Hz) + A0 (27.5 Hz) sine drones, looped</td></tr>
</table>

<p>The <code>AudioContext</code> is created on the first user gesture (<kbd>click</kbd> / <kbd>keydown</kbd>) per browser autoplay policy. Volume is controlled by <code>GameState.settings</code> with separate master, SFX, and music gain nodes.</p>
</section>

<!-- ── Rendering ─────────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="rendering">
<h2>Rendering Pipeline</h2>
<p>The <code>RenderManager</code> draws in this order each frame (after the camera transform is applied):</p>

<ol>
  <li><strong>Sky gradient</strong> — deep-space black to horizon blue, shifts with camera Y</li>
  <li><strong>Mountains</strong> — two parallax layers (depth 0.5 / 0.7), jagged silhouettes</li>
  <li><strong>Clouds</strong> — 30 ellipses at parallax depth 0.15–0.35</li>
  <li><strong>Ground line</strong> — subtle glow + grid</li>
  <li><strong>Blocks</strong> — coloured by material, frustum-culled, 3-px bevel, stress red-tint overlay</li>
  <li><strong>Stress heatmap</strong> — constraint lines coloured green→yellow→red based on <code>|reaction| / maxForce</code></li>
  <li><strong>Snap particles</strong> — white circles that grow and fade when a weld breaks</li>
  <li><strong>Ghost preview</strong> — translucent green (valid) or red (invalid) at cursor</li>
  <li><strong>Floating text</strong> — "+$15", "-10" popups that float upward and fade out</li>
  <li><strong>Crosshair</strong> — subtle centre-screen indicator</li>
</ol>

<div class="callout tip">
  <strong>Performance:</strong> Blocks outside the view frustum (plus 100 px margin) are culled. Stress lines are culled if both endpoints are off-screen. Floating text is trivially cheap.
</div>
</section>

<!-- ── Save System ──────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="save">
<h2>Save System</h2>
<p>Saves are written to <code>localStorage</code> under the key <code>tower_save</code>.</p>

<ul>
  <li><strong>Autosave</strong> every 30 seconds</li>
  <li><strong>On-unload save</strong> when the page closes</li>
  <li><strong>Manual wipe</strong> button (double-click confirmation) in the bottom-right corner</li>
</ul>

<p>The save payload includes:</p>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">json</span>{
  "schema":     1,
  "savedAt":    1712345678000,
  "playTime":   3600,
  "maxHeight":  1200,
  "gameState":  { /* full serialisable state */ },
  "modules": {
    "PhysicsEngine":    { "bodies": [...], "constraints": [...] },
    "AutomationManager": { "nextId": 42, "cooldown": 1.2 },
    ...
  }
}</pre>

<div class="callout info">
  <strong>Validation:</strong> Each load goes through a 4-step pipeline: JSON parse → schema version check → <code>isValidState()</code> structural validation → field backfill for older saves. Corrupt data is silently discarded.
</div>
</section>

<!-- ── Project Structure ────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="structure">
<h2>Project Structure</h2>
<pre><span class="lang-tag">tree</span>tower/
├── index.html              ← Entry point + CSS layout + HUD
├── README.md
└── js/
    ├── main.js             ← Bootstrap, module wiring, cross-module chains
    ├── state.js            ← GameState typedef, factory, clone, validation
    ├── constants.js        ← All tunable numbers
    ├── math.js             ← Pure scaling formulas
    ├── core/
    │   ├── GameLoop.js     ← RAF orchestrator, dt capping, phase ordering
    │   ├── InputManager.js ← Pointer/keyboard capture, ghost, camera
    │   ├── EconomyManager.js ← Income, upgrades, resource validation
    │   ├── StatTracker.js  ← Metric monitor + event emitter
    │   ├── AchievementManager.js ← Data-driven achievement checker
    │   ├── AutomationManager.js  ← Auto-builder drone
    │   ├── PhysicsEngine.js ← Matter.js wrapper, welds, wind
    │   ├── EventManager.js ← Wind gusts, micro-impulses
    │   ├── StressSolver.js ← Constraint-force stress reader
    │   ├── RenderManager.js ← Canvas 2D rendering pipeline
    │   ├── UIManager.js    ← DOM HUD + achievement toaster
    │   ├── SaveManager.js  ← localStorage persistence
    │   ├── AudioManager.js ← Web Audio API procedural sounds
    │   └── PrestigeSystem.js ← Reset + reward + multipliers
    └── data/
        ├── upgrades.json       ← 5 upgrades
        └── achievements.json   ← 20 achievements</pre>
</section>

<!-- ── Audit ───────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="audit">
<h2>Audit &amp; Known Issues</h2>
<p>The codebase was subjected to a full systems audit covering state integrity, physics memory management, math safety, and rendering performance. <strong>12 issues</strong> were identified and fixed.</p>

<h3>Critical Fixes Applied</h3>
<table>
  <tr><th>#</th><th>Issue</th><th>Fix</th></tr>
  <tr><td>1</td><td><code>EventManager.js</code>: <code>const Matter = window.Matter;</code> was inside a JSDoc <code>/** */</code> block — micro-impulse events crashed with <code>ReferenceError</code></td><td>Moved the declaration outside the comment block</td></tr>
  <tr><td>2</td><td><code>main.js</code>: StressSolver patch removed blocks from GameState but never called <code>physics.destroyBlock()</code> — orphan Matter bodies leaked on every collapse</td><td>Added <code>physics.destroyBlock(blockId)</code> before GameState removal</td></tr>
  <tr><td>3</td><td><code>PhysicsEngine.deserialize()</code>: Created a new ground body each save-load without removing the old one — accumulating duplicate grounds</td><td>Added <code>Composite.remove()</code> of old ground before rebuilding</td></tr>
  <tr><td>4</td><td><code>main.js</code> + <code>GameLoop.js</code>: SaveManager was never registered in the phase list — autosave timer searched for a phase named <code>'SaveManager'</code> that didn't exist</td><td>Added <code>loop.register({name:'SaveManager', ...})</code> to the phase list</td></tr>
</table>

<h3>High / Medium Fixes</h3>
<table>
  <tr><th>#</th><th>Issue</th><th>Fix</th></tr>
  <tr><td>5</td><td><code>main.js</code>: <code>input._placeBlock</code> was completely replaced (duplicating all placement logic) instead of wrapping the original</td><td>Changed to call <code>origPlaceBlock()</code> then inject hooks</td></tr>
  <tr><td>6</td><td><code>main.js</code>: Used <code>ui._short()</code> — a private UIManager method, breaking encapsulation</td><td>Moved <code>formatNumber</code>/<code>formatShort</code> to <code>math.js</code> as exported functions, imported by both UIManager and main.js</td></tr>
  <tr><td>7</td><td><code>main.js</code>: Same replacement pattern for <code>automation._autoPlaceBlock</code></td><td>Changed to wrapper pattern</td></tr>
  <tr><td>8</td><td><code>EconomyManager.js</code>: Height factor was additive in income formula (income started at 2× at height 0)</td><td>Changed to multiplicative: <code>base × prestige × heightFactor × (1 + upgradeBonus)</code></td></tr>
  <tr><td>9</td><td><code>PhysicsEngine._cullFallenBlocks()</code>: Incremented <code>totalCollapses</code> for harmless debris removal</td><td>Removed the increment (collapses are tracked by StressSolver only)</td></tr>
  <tr><td>10</td><td><code>UIManager._eng(n)</code>: Returned <code>"Infinityundefined"</code> for NaN inputs</td><td>Delegated to <code>formatNumber()</code> from <code>math.js</code> which has a <code>!Number.isFinite</code> guard</td></tr>
  <tr><td>11</td><td><code>math.js costExponential()</code>: Overflows to <code>Infinity</code> at extreme upgrade levels</td><td>Added <code>!Number.isFinite(result)</code> guard returning <code>MAX_SAFE_INTEGER</code></td></tr>
  <tr><td>12</td><td><code>AchievementManager.js</code>: "Self-Aware" referenced <code>state.stats.otherAchievements</code> which doesn't exist</td><td>Added <code>other_achievements</code> condition type counting unlocked achievements</td></tr>
</table>

<div class="callout tip">
  <strong>Architecture Invariants Preserved:</strong> Single source of truth (shared <code>GameState</code>), strict 11-phase GameLoop ordering, deterministic pure-function math, safe persistence with silent corruption handling, and decoupled cross-module communication via GameState mutation + the StatTracker event bus.
</div>
</section>

<!-- ── Development ───────────────────────────────────────────── -->
<section id="development">
<h2>Development Guide</h2>

<h3>Adding an Upgrade</h3>
<ol>
  <li>Add its definition to <code>js/data/upgrades.json</code> AND the <code>UPGRADE_DEFS</code> array in <code>EconomyManager.js</code>.</li>
  <li>Use <code>economy.getEffectValue('your_effect_type')</code> in the consuming module.</li>
</ol>

<h3>Adding an Achievement</h3>
<ol>
  <li>Add its definition to <code>js/data/achievements.json</code> AND the <code>ACHIEVEMENT_DEFS</code> array in <code>AchievementManager.js</code>.</li>
  <li>Available condition types: <code>stat_ge</code>, <code>max_height_ge</code>, <code>prestige_count</code>, <code>upgrade_level</code>.</li>
  <li>Stats emitted by <code>StatTracker</code>: <code>blocks_placed</code>, <code>money_earned</code>, <code>steel_earned</code>, <code>research_earned</code>, <code>collapse</code>, <code>upgrade_purchased</code>, <code>prestige</code>, <code>max_height</code>.</li>
</ol>

<h3>Module Conventions</h3>
<p>Every module follows the same interface:</p>
<ul>
  <li><code>constructor(...dependencies)</code> — receives external refs</li>
  <li><code>init(state)</code> — receives shared <code>GameState</code>, builds internal structures</li>
  <li><code>update(dt)</code> — per-frame logic (if registered in GameLoop)</li>
  <li><code>serialize()</code> — returns module-specific data or <code>null</code></li>
  <li><code>deserialize(data, state)</code> — restores from serialized data</li>
</ul>

<h3>Tech Stack</h3>
<table>
  <tr><th>Layer</th><th>Technology</th></tr>
  <tr><td>Physics</td><td><a href="https://brm.io/matter-js/" target="_blank">Matter.js</a> 0.20.0</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Rendering</td><td>HTML5 Canvas 2D</td></tr>
  <tr><td>UI</td><td>Vanilla DOM (CSS Grid / Flexbox)</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Audio</td><td>Web Audio API (procedural synthesis)</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Persistence</td><td>localStorage</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Modules</td><td>ES6 (<code>import</code> / <code>export</code>)</td></tr>
  <tr><td>Dependencies</td><td>None — Matter.js loaded from CDN</td></tr>
</table>

<hr>
<p style="text-align:center;color:#4a5a6a;font-size:13px;margin-top:40px">
  Built in 7 phases across ~6,000 lines of vanilla JavaScript.
</p>
</section>

<script>
  // ── Active sidebar link tracking ──────────────────────────────
  const sections = document.querySelectorAll('section[id]');
  const links = document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a');

  function updateActiveLink() {
    let current = '';
    for (const section of sections) {
      const rect = section.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (rect.top <= 120) current = section.id;
    }
    for (const link of links) {
      link.classList.toggle('active', link.getAttribute('href') === '#' + current);
    }
  }

  window.addEventListener('scroll', updateActiveLink);
  window.addEventListener('load', updateActiveLink);

  // ── Smooth scroll for sidebar clicks ──────────────────────────
  for (const link of links) {
    link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      const id = link.getAttribute('href').slice(1);
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el) el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
    });
  }
</script>

<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/matter-js/0.20.0/matter.min.js"></script>
<script>
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// TOWER BUILDER — v8 (pinned base, tunable strength, robust collapse detect)
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//
// FIX: First layer is now STATIC (pinned to ground). This prevents the
//   whole tower from sliding sideways when it sways. The base acts as
//   a pivot point for natural toppling.
//
// FIX: strBase reduced to 120+upLvl*50 (was 400+upLvl*140). Constraints
//   now break at ~8-10 layers without upgrades, ~30 layers with max upgrades.
//   This gives meaningful gameplay — the tower GROWS until it exceeds
//   material strength, then topples.
//
// FIX: Collapse detection uses MULTIPLE robust triggers:
//   - Height drop: if maxH falls >15% → collapse (catches ALL failures)
//   - Angular velocity: any layer > 2 rad/s → collapse
//   - Horizontal displacement: any layer > 10x SP from center → collapse
//   - Constraint breaks: >2 breaks in recent frames → collapse
//   These are OBSERVABLE behaviors, not dependent on reaction force accuracy.

const Me=window.Matter;
let G=3;
const SP=43, PH=21, BH=18, BD=43;
const GRAV=0.6;
const POS_ITERS=30, VEL_ITERS=22, CON_ITERS=18;
const EDGE_STIFF=0.97, CENTER_STIFF=0.93, JOINT_DAMP=0.5;
const STRESS_SNAP=0.97;
const FALL_CULL=25000;

let money=50, maxH=0, stressPct=0;
let upLvl=0, spdLvl=0, sizeLvl=0;
let placeInterval=0.025;
let nextId=1;
const layers=[], constraints=new Map();
let layerCount=0, activeBricks=0;
let currentLayerIdx=-1, currentBricksPlaced=0;
let collapsing=false, breakCount=0, collapseNotified=false;
// Height tracking for drop detection
let prevMaxH=maxH, heightDropTimer=0;

function strBase(){return 120+upLvl*50} // ~8-10 layers base, 30+ with upgrades
function getOFF(){return ((G-1)*SP)/2}

// ── Matter.js ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const engine=Me.Engine.create({
  gravity:{x:0,y:GRAV},
  positionIterations:POS_ITERS,velocityIterations:VEL_ITERS,constraintIterations:CON_ITERS
});
Me.Composite.add(engine.world,Me.Bodies.rectangle(0,25,30000,50,{
  isStatic:true,label:'ground',
  friction:1.0,frictionStatic:1.0,restitution:0,
  collisionFilter:{category:0x0001}
}));

// ── Three.js ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const R=new THREE.WebGLRenderer({antialias:true});
R.setSize(innerWidth,innerHeight);
R.setPixelRatio(Math.min(devicePixelRatio,2));
R.setClearColor(0x0b0f1e,1);
R.shadowMap.enabled=true;R.shadowMap.type=THREE.PCFSoftShadowMap;
document.body.prepend(R.domElement);
const S=new THREE.Scene();S.fog=new THREE.Fog(0x0b0f1e,6000,12000);
const C=new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(45,innerWidth/innerHeight,1,30000);
S.add(new THREE.AmbientLight(0x404060,0.5));
S.add(new THREE.HemisphereLight(0x87ceeb,0x362d59,0.3));
const s=new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffeedd,1.0);
s.position.set(400,600,300);s.castShadow=true;
s.shadow.mapSize.set(4096,4096);
s.shadow.camera.near=1;s.shadow.camera.far=3000;
s.shadow.camera.left=-1500;s.shadow.camera.right=1500;
s.shadow.camera.top=1500;s.shadow.camera.bottom=-1500;
S.add(s);const f=new THREE.DirectionalLight(0x8888ff,0.3);
f.position.set(-200,100,-300);S.add(f);
const W=new THREE.Group();S.add(W);
const g=new THREE.GridHelper(8000,80,0x152040,0x0a1020);
g.position.y=-2;W.add(g);

// ── Layer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function createLayerBody(li){
  const id=nextId++, y=-PH/2-li*PH;
  // First layer is STATIC — pinned to ground, acts as pivot
  const isBase=(li===0);
  const b=Me.Bodies.rectangle(0,y,G*SP,PH,{
    density:(G*G)*0.001,friction:0.8,frictionStatic:0.8,
    frictionAir:0.008,restitution:0,label:'L'+li,
    isStatic:isBase, // FIX: base layer is pinned
    collisionFilter:{group:-1,category:0x0001,mask:0x0001}
  });
  b._layerId=li;b._towerId=id;
  Me.Composite.add(engine.world,b);
  const e={id,body:b,meshes:[],layerIdx:li,alive:true,y,stress:0};
  layers.push(e);return e;
}
function addMesh(le,ix,iz){
  const OFF=getOFF(),mx=ix*SP-OFF,mz=iz*SP-OFF,BW=SP*0.95;
  const m=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(BW,BH,BD),
    new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x888888,roughness:0.6,metalness:0.2,emissive:0x000000,emissiveIntensity:0.6}));
  m.position.set(mx,-le.y+BH,mz);m.castShadow=true;m.receiveShadow=true;
  m._ix=ix;m._iz=iz;W.add(m);le.meshes.push(m);activeBricks++;
}
function connectLayer(le){
  if(layers.length<2)return;
  const lo=layers[layers.length-2];
  if(!lo||!lo.alive)return;
  // Center: axial, connects body centers, length=PH
  {const con=Me.Constraint.create({
    bodyA:le.body,bodyB:lo.body,
    pointA:{x:0,y:0},pointB:{x:0,y:0},
    stiffness:CENTER_STIFF,damping:JOINT_DAMP,length:PH
  });con._maxForce=strBase()*1.5;con._towerIds=[le.id,lo.id];con._layerIdx=le.layerIdx;con._isCenter=true;
  constraints.set(le.id+'_'+lo.id+'_1',{con,layerIdx:le.layerIdx,isCenter:true});
  Me.Composite.add(engine.world,con);}
  // LEFT edge: length=0
  {const con=Me.Constraint.create({
    bodyA:le.body,bodyB:lo.body,
    pointA:{x:-SP,y:PH/2},pointB:{x:-SP,y:-PH/2},
    stiffness:EDGE_STIFF,damping:JOINT_DAMP,length:0
  });con._maxForce=strBase();con._towerIds=[le.id,lo.id];con._layerIdx=le.layerIdx;
  constraints.set(le.id+'_'+lo.id+'_0',{con,layerIdx:le.layerIdx});
  Me.Composite.add(engine.world,con);}
  // RIGHT edge: length=0
  {const con=Me.Constraint.create({
    bodyA:le.body,bodyB:lo.body,
    pointA:{x:SP,y:PH/2},pointB:{x:SP,y:-PH/2},
    stiffness:EDGE_STIFF,damping:JOINT_DAMP,length:0
  });con._maxForce=strBase();con._towerIds=[le.id,lo.id];con._layerIdx=le.layerIdx;
  constraints.set(le.id+'_'+lo.id+'_2',{con,layerIdx:le.layerIdx});
  Me.Composite.add(engine.world,con);}
}
function placeBrick(){
  if(collapsing)return;
  const total=G*G;
  if(currentLayerIdx<0||currentBricksPlaced>=total){
    currentLayerIdx=layerCount;currentBricksPlaced=0;
    connectLayer(createLayerBody(layerCount));layerCount++;
  }
  const e=layers[currentLayerIdx];
  if(!e||!e.alive)return;
  addMesh(e,currentBricksPlaced%G,Math.floor(currentBricksPlaced/G));
  currentBricksPlaced++;
}

// ── Stress + Robust Collapse Detection ────────────────────────────────
function solveStress(dt){
  let maxS=0, newBreaks=0;
  const brokenSet=new Set();

  for(const[_,e]of constraints){
    if(!e||!e.con||!e.con.reaction||e.con._broken)continue;
    const c=e.con;
    const mag=Math.sqrt(c.reaction.x**2+c.reaction.y**2);
    const th=c._maxForce||100;
    const r=mag/th;
    if(r>maxS)maxS=r;
    if(r>0.7){c._fat=(c._fat||0)+dt;if(c._fat>1){c._fat-=1;c._maxForce*=0.98;}}
    else c._fat=Math.max(0,(c._fat||0)-dt*0.5);
    if(r>STRESS_SNAP){c._broken=true;Me.Composite.remove(engine.world,c);newBreaks++;brokenSet.add(c._layerIdx);}
  }
  for(const[_,e]of constraints){
    if(!e||!e.con||e.con._broken)continue;
    if(brokenSet.has(e.layerIdx)){e.con._maxForce*=0.90;e.con._fat=(e.con._fat||0)+0.3;}
  }
  // Angle-based stress
  for(const l of layers){
    if(!l.alive)continue;
    l.stress=Math.min(1.5,Math.max(Math.abs(l.body.angle)/0.15,l.stress||0));
  }

  // ── ROBUST COLLAPSE DETECTION ──
  // Multiple independent triggers, any one can fire:
  let collapse=false;
  // 1. Height drop >15% in 2 seconds
  heightDropTimer+=dt;
  if(heightDropTimer>2){heightDropTimer=0;
    if(prevMaxH>50&&maxH<prevMaxH*0.85)collapse=true;
    prevMaxH=maxH;
  }
  // 2. Any layer spinning or flying
  let maxAV=0,maxLV=0,maxDX=0;
  for(const l of layers){
    if(!l.alive||l.body.isStatic)continue;
    const av=Math.abs(l.body.angularVelocity);
    const lv=Math.sqrt(l.body.velocity.x**2+l.body.velocity.y**2);
    const dx=Math.abs(l.body.position.x);
    if(av>maxAV)maxAV=av;if(lv>maxLV)maxLV=lv;if(dx>maxDX)maxDX=dx;
  }
  if(maxAV>2||maxLV>50||maxDX>SP*10)collapse=true;
  // 3. Multiple constraint breaks
  breakCount+=newBreaks;breakCount*=0.95;
  if(breakCount>3)collapse=true;
  // 4. Stress > 99%
  if(maxS>0.99)collapse=true;

  if(!collapsing&&collapse){
    collapsing=true;
    if(!collapseNotified){collapseNotified=true;toast('💥 COLLAPSE — Tower has fallen!','bad');}
  }

  // Cull fallen layers
  for(let i=layers.length-1;i>=0;i--){
    const l=layers[i];if(!l||!l.alive||l.body.isStatic)continue;
    if(l.body.position.y>FALL_CULL){
      l.alive=false;
      for(const[_,ce]of constraints){
        if(ce&&ce.con&&!ce.con._broken&&(ce.con._towerIds||[]).includes(l.id)){
          ce.con._broken=true;Me.Composite.remove(engine.world,ce.con);}}
      for(const m of(l.meshes||[])){if(m.parent)W.remove(m);m.geometry.dispose();m.material.dispose();}
      l.meshes=[];Me.Composite.remove(engine.world,l.body);
    }
  }
  let ty=0;for(const l of layers){if(l.alive){const h=-l.body.position.y+BH;if(h>ty)ty=h;}}
  maxH=ty;stressPct=Math.min(100,Math.round(maxS*100));
}

// ── Colors ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function updateColors(){
  for(const l of layers){
    if(!l.alive)continue;
    const s=l.stress||0;let r=0x66,g=0x66,b=0x66;
    if(s>0.15){const t=Math.min(1,(s-0.15)/0.85);
      if(t<0.25){const u=t/0.25;r=0x66*(1-u)+0x44*u;g=0x66*(1-u)+0x88*u;b=0x66*(1-u)+0xcc*u;}
      else if(t<0.5){const u=(t-0.25)/0.25;r=0x44*(1-u)+0x22*u;g=0x88*(1-u)+0xcc*u;b=0xcc*(1-u)+0x66*u;}
      else if(t<0.75){const u=(t-0.5)/0.25;r=0x22*(1-u)+0xee*u;g=0xcc*(1-u)+0xaa*u;b=0x66*(1-u)+0x22*u;}
      else{const u=(t-0.75)/0.25;r=0xee*(1-u)+0xff*u;g=0xaa*(1-u)+0x44*u;b=0x22*(1-u);}
    }
    r=Math.min(255,Math.max(0,Math.floor(r)));g=Math.min(255,Math.max(0,Math.floor(g)));b=Math.min(255,Math.max(0,Math.floor(b)));
    const col=(r<<16)+(g<<8)+b,em=Math.min(s*3,1);
    const eh=(Math.min(255,r*em)<<16)+(Math.min(255,g*em*0.6)<<8)+Math.min(255,b*em*0.3);
    for(const m of(l.meshes||[])){if(m.material){m.material.color.setHex(col);m.material.emissive.setHex(eh);m.material.emissiveIntensity=0.3+s*0.6;}}
  }
}

// ── Sync ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function sync3D(){
  for(const l of layers){
    if(!l.alive)continue;
    const bx=l.body.position.x,by=l.body.position.y,ang=l.body.angle;
    const ca=Math.cos(ang),sa=Math.sin(ang),OFF=getOFF();
    for(const m of(l.meshes||[])){
      const mx=m._ix*SP-OFF,mz=m._iz*SP-OFF;
      m.position.set(bx+mx*ca,-by+BH-mx*sa,mz);m.rotation.z=-ang;
    }
  }
}

// ── Wind ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
let wPhase=0,wDir=1,wAcc=0;
function windTick(dt){
  wPhase+=dt*0.3;if(Math.random()<0.015)wDir*=-1;
  const gust=Math.sin(wPhase*Math.PI*2)*0.4+0.6;
  const str=0.0002*(1+(maxH||1)/200)*gust;
  for(const l of layers){
    if(!l.alive||l.body.isStatic)continue;
    Me.Body.applyForce(l.body,l.body.position,{x:str*wDir*(1+Math.max(0,-l.body.position.y)/300)*300,y:0});
  }
}
function earn(dt){money+=2*(1+maxH/30)*(1+upLvl*0.08)*dt;}

// ── Camera ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
let theta=0.7,phi=0.5,dist=2000,panX=0,panZ=0;
let drag=false,dl={},panning=false,ps={},pc={};
function cam(){
  const ty=Math.max(30,maxH*0.35),td=Math.max(1400,Math.min(30000,maxH*0.6+800));
  dist+=(td-dist)*0.04;
  C.position.set(dist*Math.sin(theta)*Math.cos(phi)+panX,Math.max(100,dist*Math.sin(phi)+150),dist*Math.cos(theta)*Math.cos(phi)+panZ);
  C.lookAt(panX,ty,panZ);
}

// ── HUD ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function toast(m,t){
  const e=document.createElement('div');e.className='tt '+(t||'');e.textContent=m;
  document.getElementById('tt').appendChild(e);setTimeout(function(){if(e.parentNode)e.parentNode.removeChild(e)},3000);
}
function updateHUD(){
  document.getElementById('h-h').textContent=Math.floor(maxH);
  document.getElementById('h-b').textContent=activeBricks;
  document.getElementById('h-$').textContent=Math.floor(money);
  const se=document.getElementById('h-s');
  se.textContent=collapsing?'☠ COLLAPSE':stressPct+'%';
  se.style.color=collapsing?'#f44':stressPct<40?'#8c8':stressPct<75?'#cc8':'#f88';
}
let hudTimer=0;
function buyJoint(){
  if(collapsing){toast('Nope — collapsing!','bad');return;}
  const cost=80*Math.pow(1.5,upLvl);
  if(money<cost){toast('Need $'+Math.ceil(cost),'bad');return;}if(upLvl>=25){toast('Max!','blue');return;}
  money-=cost;upLvl++;toast('⬆ Joint Lv'+upLvl+' +'+(upLvl*50)+' strength','blue');updateHUD();
}
function buySpeed(){
  if(collapsing){toast('Nope — collapsing!','bad');return;}
  const cost=10*Math.pow(2,spdLvl);
  if(money<cost){toast('Need $'+Math.ceil(cost),'bad');return;}if(spdLvl>=15){toast('Max!','blue');return;}
  money-=cost;spdLvl++;placeInterval=Math.max(0.005,placeInterval-0.002);
  toast('⚡ Speed Lv'+spdLvl+' '+Math.round(placeInterval*1000)+'ms','blue');updateHUD();
}
function buyBigger(){
  if(collapsing){toast('Nope — collapsing!','bad');return;}
  const cost=500*Math.pow(3,sizeLvl);
  if(money<cost){toast('Need $'+Math.ceil(cost),'bad');return;}if(sizeLvl>=4){toast('Max!','blue');return;}
  money-=cost;sizeLvl++;G=3+sizeLvl;toast('🏗️ '+G+'×'+G,'blue');updateHUD();
}
document.getElementById('b-up').onclick=buyJoint;
document.getElementById('b-spd').onclick=buySpeed;
document.getElementById('b-big').onclick=buyBigger;
document.getElementById('b-r').onclick=function(){theta=0.7;phi=0.5;dist=2000;panX=0;panZ=0;};

R.domElement.addEventListener('pointerdown',function(e){
  if(e.button===1||e.button===2){drag=true;dl={x:e.clientX,y:e.clientY};e.preventDefault();}
  else if(e.button===0&&e.shiftKey){panning=true;ps={x:e.clientX,y:e.clientY};pc={x:panX,z:panZ};}
});
document.addEventListener('pointerup',function(ev){if(!ev.buttons){drag=false;panning=false;}});
document.addEventListener('pointermove',function(e){
  if(panning){panX=pc.x-(e.clientX-ps.x)*0.5;panZ=pc.z-(e.clientY-ps.y)*0.5;return;}
  if(drag){theta-=(e.clientX-dl.x)*0.005;phi=Math.max(0.1,Math.min(1.3,phi+(e.clientY-dl.y)*0.005));dl={x:e.clientX,y:e.clientY};}
});
R.domElement.addEventListener('wheel',function(e){e.preventDefault();dist=Math.max(600,Math.min(20000,dist*(e.deltaY<0?0.9:1.1)));},{passive:false});
addEventListener('resize',function(){C.aspect=innerWidth/innerHeight;C.updateProjectionMatrix();R.setSize(innerWidth,innerHeight);});
addEventListener('keydown',function(e){
  if(e.code==='KeyC'||e.code==='Escape'){theta=0.7;phi=0.5;dist=2000;panX=0;panZ=0;}
  if(e.code==='KeyU')buyJoint();
});

placeBrick();
toast('🧱 Tower building...','blue');

let last=0,acc=0,ct=0;
function loop(t){
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  const dt=last?Math.min((t-last)/1000,0.05):0.016;last=t;
  if(!collapsing){acc+=dt;if(acc>=placeInterval){acc=0;placeBrick();}}
  wAcc+=dt;if(!collapsing&&wAcc>3){wAcc=0;windTick(dt);}
  Me.Engine.update(engine,dt*1000);
  for(const l of layers){if(l.alive&&!l.body.isStatic)Me.Body.setAngularVelocity(l.body,l.body.angularVelocity*0.95);}
  solveStress(dt);if(!collapsing)earn(dt);sync3D();
  ct+=dt;if(ct>0.1){ct=0;updateColors();}
  cam();hudTimer+=dt;if(hudTimer>0.15){hudTimer=0;updateHUD();}
  R.render(S,C);
}
loop(0);
console.log('[Tower] v8 — pinned base, strBase='+strBase()+', multi-trigger collapse');
</script>
</body></html>

/**
 * constants.js
 * ------------
 * Central configuration constants for Tower.
 * All tunable numbers live here so they can be tweaked without hunting.
 */

export const CONFIG = Object.freeze({

  // ── Timing ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  TICK_CAP_S: 0.050,            // Cap delta-time at 50 ms to avoid spiral-of-death
  UI_THROTTLE_FRAMES: 5,        // Update DOM every N frames
  AUTOSAVE_INTERVAL_MS: 30_000,

  // ── Economy ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  STARTING_MONEY: 100,
  STARTING_STEEL: 10,
  STARTING_RESEARCH: 0,

  BLOCK_BASE_COST: 10,          // base money cost per block placed

  INCOME_BASE_MONEY: 1,         // money per second before any multipliers
  INCOME_BASE_STEEL: 0.1,       // steel per second before multipliers
  INCOME_BASE_RESEARCH: 0.05,   // research per second before multipliers
  INCOME_HEIGHT_SCALE: 100,     // every N height units doubles income factor

  OFFLINE_CHUNK_S: 1,           // simulate 1 s per chunk during offline catch-up
  OFFLINE_MAX_S: 3600,          // cap offline catch-up at 1 hour

  // ── Tower ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  BLOCK_WIDTH: 60,
  BLOCK_HEIGHT: 20,
  BLOCK_STACK_SPACING: 2,       // vertical gap between blocks
  MAX_BLOCKS_PER_TIER: 8,

  // ── Placement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  GRID_SNAP_SIZE: 10,           // default grid resolution (world units)
  PLACEMENT_SUPPORT_TOLERANCE: 14, // how close block bottom must be to support
  GHOST_ALPHA_VALID: 0.45,      // opacity of ghost when valid
  GHOST_ALPHA_INVALID: 0.20,    // opacity of ghost when invalid

  // ── Physics (Matter.js tuning) ────────────────────────────────────────────
  GRAVITY_Y: 1.0,
  POSITION_ITERATIONS: 6,
  VELOCITY_ITERATIONS: 4,
  CONSTRAINT_ITERATIONS: 2,

  // ── Stress ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  STRESS_PER_BLOCK: 0.10,       // stress added per supported block above
  STRESS_BREAK_THRESHOLD: 1.0,  // block breaks when stress >= 1.0
  STRESS_DISSIPATE_RATE: 0.02,  // per-second decay when no new load added

  // ── Camera ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  CAMERA_MIN_ZOOM: 0.1,
  CAMERA_MAX_ZOOM: 4.0,
  CAMERA_DEFAULT_ZOOM: 1.0,
  CAMERA_LERP: 0.08,            // smoothing factor for follow-target
  CAMERA_PAN_BOUNDARY: 5000,    // max X/Y distance camera can pan from origin

  // ── Prestige ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  PRESTIGE_MIN_HEIGHT: 500,     // minimum maxHeight required to prestige
  PRESTIGE_REWARD_SCALE: 0.5,   // reward = floor(sqrt(maxHeight * scale))
  PRESTIGE_MULT_PER_TOKEN: 0.10, // +10 % income per prestige token held

  // ── Save ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  SAVE_KEY: 'tower_save',
  SAVE_VERSION: 1,

  // ── Automation ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  AUTO_BUILDER_INTERVAL_S: 2.0, // base interval between auto-placements (s)
  // ── Audio ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  MASTER_VOLUME: 0.5,           // 0–1 global volume
  SFX_VOLUME: 0.7,             // sound-effects volume multiplier
  MUSIC_VOLUME: 0.3,           // background-music volume multiplier
  PITCH_VARIANCE: 0.15,        // ±15 % random pitch shift for sfx variety
  MUSIC_ENABLED: true,          // background music on by default
});

File: js/core/AchievementManager.js

/**
 * AchievementManager.js
 * ---------------------
 * Data-driven achievement system.
 *
 * Achievements are defined in ACHIEVEMENT_DEFS (inlined below, mirrored
 * from js/data/achievements.json).  Each achievement has a condition
 * object that is checked against GameState and cumulative stats.
 *
 * Checking flow:
 *   1. StatTracker emits a change event → AchievementManager.onStatEvent()
 *   2. The event is matched against all locked achievements.
 *   3. If a condition passes, the achievement is unlocked and stored in
 *      GameState.achievements.unlocked.
 *   4. An 'unlock' event is dispatched to the callback (used by UIManager
 *      to show the notification toaster).
 *
 * Condition types:
 *   stat_ge          → state.stats[stat] >= threshold
 *   max_height_ge    → state.tower.maxHeight >= threshold
 *   prestige_count   → state.prestige.resetCount >= threshold
 *   upgrade_ge       → (state.upgrades[id]?.level ?? 0) >= threshold
 *
 * Persistence:
 *   Unlocked achievement IDs are stored in GameState.achievements.unlocked,
 *   which is serialised as part of the normal save cycle.
 */

/** @typedef {import('../state.js').GameState} GameState */

/**
 * @typedef {Object} AchievementDef
 * @property {string} id
 * @property {string} name
 * @property {string} description
 * @property {string} icon
 * @property {{ type: string, stat?: string, threshold: number }} condition
 */

export class AchievementManager {

  constructor() {
    /** @type {Map<string, AchievementDef>} */
    this._defs = new Map();

    /** @type {GameState|null} */
    this._state = null;

    /** @type {Function|null}  — callback(achievementDef) called on unlock */
    this._onUnlock = null;

    /** @type {Set<string>}  — cached unlocked set for O(1) lookups */
    this._unlocked = new Set();
  }

  /* ── Lifecycle ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  /**
   * @param {GameState} state
   */
  init(state) {
    this._state = state;
    this._defs = new Map(ACHIEVEMENT_DEFS.map((a) => [a.id, a]));

    // Populate unlocked set from saved state
    if (state.achievements?.unlocked) {
      for (const id of state.achievements.unlocked) {
        this._unlocked.add(id);
      }
    }
  }

  /**
   * No per-frame work — we react to StatTracker events.
   * @param {number} dt
   */
  update(dt) {
    // All checking is event-driven
  }

  /* ── Event handler (called by StatTracker) ─────────────────────────── */

  /**
   * Called by StatTracker when a cumulative stat changes.
   * Scans all locked achievements and unlocks any whose conditions are met.
   *
   * @param {GameState} state
   * @param {string} event  — e.g. 'blocks_placed', 'money_earned', etc.
   * @param {object} data
   */
  onStatEvent(state, event, data) {
    if (!this._state) return;
    const newlyUnlocked = [];

    for (const [id, def] of this._defs) {
      if (this._unlocked.has(id)) continue;

      if (this._checkCondition(def.condition, state, data)) {
        this._unlock(id, def);
        newlyUnlocked.push(def);
      }
    }

    // Fire callbacks for each new unlock
    for (const def of newlyUnlocked) {
      if (this._onUnlock) this._onUnlock(def);
    }
  }

  /* ── Condition checking ────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  /**
   * Test a single condition against the current state.
   *
   * @param {{ type: string, stat?: string, id?: string, threshold: number }} cond
   * @param {GameState} state
   * @param {object} eventData  — additional data from the stat change event
   * @returns {boolean}
   */
  _checkCondition(cond, state, eventData) {
    switch (cond.type) {
      case 'stat_ge': {
        const val = state.stats[cond.stat];
        return val != null && val >= cond.threshold;
      }
      case 'max_height_ge': {
        return state.tower.maxHeight >= cond.threshold;
      }
      case 'prestige_count': {
        return state.prestige.resetCount >= cond.threshold;
      }
      case 'upgrade_level': {
        const level = state.upgrades[cond.id]?.level ?? 0;
        return level >= cond.threshold;
      }
      // Count achievements unlocked (used for "Self-Aware" meta-achievement)
      case 'other_achievements': {
        const unlocked = state.achievements?.unlocked?.length ?? 0;
        return unlocked >= cond.threshold;
      }
      default:
        return false;
    }
  }

  /* ── Internal ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  /**
   * Mark an achievement as unlocked and persist.
   * @param {string} id
   * @param {AchievementDef} def
   */
  _unlock(id, def) {
    this._unlocked.add(id);

    // Ensure the array exists in state
    if (!this._state.achievements) {
      this._state.achievements = { unlocked: [] };
    }
    if (!this._state.achievements.unlocked.includes(id)) {
      this._state.achievements.unlocked.push(id);
    }
  }

  /* ── Queries ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  /**
   * Check if a specific achievement is unlocked.
   * @param {string} id
   * @returns {boolean}
   */
  isUnlocked(id) {
    return this._unlocked.has(id);
  }

  /**
   * Get the definition for an achievement ID.
   * @param {string} id
   * @returns {AchievementDef|undefined}
   */
  getDef(id) {
    return this._defs.get(id);
  }

  /**
   * Get all achievement definitions (for UI display).
   * @returns {IterableIterator<AchievementDef>}
   */
  getAllDefs() {
    return this._defs.values();
  }

  /**
   * Get the count of unlocked achievements.
   * @returns {number}
   */
  getUnlockedCount() {
    return this._unlocked.size;
  }

  /**
   * Get total number of achievements.
   * @returns {number}
   */
  getTotalCount() {
    return this._defs.size;
  }

  /**
   * Register an unlock callback.
   * @param {Function} fn  — fn(achievementDef)
   */
  onUnlock(fn) {
    this._onUnlock = fn;
  }

  /* ── Serialization ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  serialize() {
    return null; // state lives in GameState.achievements
  }

  /**
   * @param {object|null} data
   * @param {GameState} state
   */
  deserialize(data, state) {
    this._state = state;
    this._unlocked.clear();
    if (state.achievements?.unlocked) {
      for (const id of state.achievements.unlocked) {
        this._unlocked.add(id);
      }
    }
  }
}

 *

/**
 * AudioManager.js
 * ---------------
 * Procedural sound engine using the Web Audio API.
 *
 * All sounds are synthesised at runtime — no external audio files needed.
 * This keeps the deployable small and avoids CORS / preload headaches.
 *
 * Architecture:
 *   - Single AudioContext created on first user gesture (browser policy).
 *   - Sounds are short-lived oscillator + gain-envelope bursts.
 *   - Pitch variance (±PITCH_VARIANCE) is applied per-play to reduce
 *     the repetitive "machine gun" effect.
 *   - Volume settings live in GameState.settings and are read each play.
 *
 * Sound types:
 *   block_place   — low thud  (80 Hz square, fast decay)
 *   ui_click      — short tick (1200 Hz sine, very fast decay)
 *   collapse      — crunch     (noise + low sine, medium decay)
 *   achievement   — chime      (ascending two-tone)
 *   ambiance      — low drone  (sine + sub, looped)
 */

import { CONFIG } from '../constants.js';

/** @typedef {import('../state.js').GameState} GameState */

export class AudioManager {

  constructor() {
    /** @type {AudioContext|null} */
    this._ctx = null;

    /** @type {GameState|null} */
    this._state = null;

    /** @type {boolean} */
    this._started = false;

    /** @type {OscillatorNode|null}  — ambience loop, if active */
    this._ambience = null;

    /** @type {GainNode|null}  — master volume bus */
    this._masterGain = null;

    /** @type {GainNode|null}  — sfx sub-bus */
    this._sfxGain = null;

    /** @type {GainNode|null}  — music sub-bus */
    this._musicGain = null;
  }

  /* ── Lifecycle ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  /**
   * @param {GameState} state
   */
  init(state) {
    this._state = state;
  }

  /**
   * No per-frame work needed.
   * @param {number} dt
   */
  update(dt) {
    // nothing per-frame
  }

  /**
   * Initialise the AudioContext and gain routing.
   * Must be called from a user-gesture event (click, keydown) due to
   * browser autoplay policy.
   */
  _ensureContext() {
    if (this._ctx) return;

    this._ctx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();

    // Master volume bus
    this._masterGain = this._ctx.createGain();
    this._masterGain.gain.value = CONFIG.MASTER_VOLUME;
    this._masterGain.connect(this._ctx.destination);

    // SFX sub-bus
    this._sfxGain = this._ctx.createGain();
    this._sfxGain.gain.value = CONFIG.SFX_VOLUME;
    this._sfxGain.connect(this._masterGain);

    // Music sub-bus
    this._musicGain = this._ctx.createGain();
    this._musicGain.gain.value = CONFIG.MUSIC_VOLUME;
    this._musicGain.connect(this._masterGain);
  }

  /**
   * Call this on every user interaction to satisfy browser autoplay
   * policies.  Safe to call multiple times.
   */
  start() {
    if (this._started) return;
    this._started = true;
    this._ensureContext();
    this._startAmbience();
  }

  /* ── Public sound triggers ──────────────────────────────────────────── */

  /** Play a short low thud (block placement). */
  playBlockPlace() {
    this._ensureContext();
    const ctx = this._ctx;
    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    const pitch = 80 + Math.random() * 40;

    const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
    const gain = ctx.createGain();
    osc.type = 'sine';
    osc.frequency.value = pitch;
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0.4, now);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, now + 0.12);
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(this._sfxGain);
    osc.start(now);
    osc.stop(now + 0.15);
  }

  /** Play a very short tick (UI clicks). */
  playUIClick() {
    this._ensureContext();
    const ctx = this._ctx;
    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    const pitch = 800 + Math.random() * 400;

    const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
    const gain = ctx.createGain();
    osc.type = 'sine';
    osc.frequency.value = pitch;
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0.15, now);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, now + 0.04);
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(this._sfxGain);
    osc.start(now);
    osc.stop(now + 0.06);
  }

  /** Play a crunch (structural collapse). */
  playCollapse() {
    this._ensureContext();
    const ctx = this._ctx;
    const now = ctx.currentTime;

    // Layer 1: low rumble
    const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
    const gain1 = ctx.createGain();
    osc.type = 'sawtooth';
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(60, now);
    osc.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(20, now + 0.4);
    gain1.gain.setValueAtTime(0.3, now);
    gain1.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, now + 0.5);
    osc.connect(gain1);
    gain1.connect(this._sfxGain);
    osc.start(now);
    osc.stop(now + 0.55);

    // Layer 2: noise burst
    const bufferSize = ctx.sampleRate * 0.3;
    const buffer = ctx.createBuffer(1, bufferSize, ctx.sampleRate);
    const data = buffer.getChannelData(0);
    for (let i = 0; i < bufferSize; i++) {
      data[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * Math.exp(-i / (bufferSize * 0.15));
    }
    const noise = ctx.createBufferSource();
    const gain2 = ctx.createGain();
    noise.buffer = buffer;
    gain2.gain.setValueAtTime(0.25, now);
    gain2.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, now + 0.35);
    noise.connect(gain2);
    gain2.connect(this._sfxGain);
    noise.start(now);
  }

  /** Play an ascending chime (achievement unlocked). */
  playAchievement() {
    this._ensureContext();
    const ctx = this._ctx;
    const now = ctx.currentTime;

    const freqs = [523, 659, 784];  // C5, E5, G5

    for (let i = 0; i < freqs.length; i++) {
      const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
      const gain = ctx.createGain();
      osc.type = 'sine';
      osc.frequency.value = freqs[i];
      const t = now + i * 0.1;
      gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);
      gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.2, t + 0.02);
      gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.4);
      osc.connect(gain);
      gain.connect(this._sfxGain);
      osc.start(t);
      osc.stop(t + 0.45);
    }
  }

  /* ── Background ambience ───────────────────────────────────────────── */

  _startAmbience() {
    if (this._ambience || !this._state?.settings?.musicEnabled) return;

    const ctx = this._ctx;
    const now = ctx.currentTime;

    // Low drone oscillator
    const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
    const gain = ctx.createGain();
    osc.type = 'sine';
    osc.frequency.value = 55; // A1
    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, now);
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.06, now + 2);
    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(this._musicGain);
    osc.start(now);

    // Sub oscillator (one octave down)
    const sub = ctx.createOscillator();
    const subGain = ctx.createGain();
    sub.type = 'sine';
    sub.frequency.value = 27.5; // A0
    subGain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, now);
    subGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.04, now + 2);
    sub.connect(subGain);
    subGain.connect(this._musicGain);
    sub.start(now);

    this._ambience = { osc, sub, gain, subGain };
  }

  _stopAmbience() {
    if (!this._ambience) return;
    const now = this._ctx.currentTime;
    this._ambience.gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, now + 0.5);
    this._ambience.subGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, now + 0.5);
    this._ambience.osc.stop(now + 0.6);
    this._ambience.sub.stop(now + 0.6);
    this._ambience = null;
  }

  /**
   * Toggle background music on/off.  Respects GameState.settings.
   * @param {boolean} [on]
   */
  toggleMusic(on) {
    if (!this._state) return;
    const enabled = on !== undefined ? on : !this._state.settings.musicEnabled;
    this._state.settings.musicEnabled = enabled;

    if (enabled) {
      this._startAmbience();
    } else {
      this._stopAmbience();
    }
  }

  /* ── Volume control ────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  /** Set master volume (0–1). */
  setMasterVolume(v) {
    if (this._masterGain) this._masterGain.gain.value = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, v));
  }

  /** Set SFX volume (0–1). */
  setSFXVolume(v) {
    if (this._sfxGain) this._sfxGain.gain.value = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, v));
  }

  /** Set music volume (0–1). */
  setMusicVolume(v) {
    if (this._musicGain) this._musicGain.gain.value = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, v));
  }

  /* ── Serialization ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── */

  serialize() {
    return null;
  }

  deserialize(data, state) {
    this._state = state || data;
  }
}



================================================================================
File: js/core/AutomationManager.js
================================================================================

/**
 * AutomationManager.js
 * --------------------
 * AI / auto-builder triggered by upgrades.
 *
 * Phase 3 in the GameLoop: after economy ticks, before physics.
 * Places blocks at the tower top center if supported and affordable.
 *
 * Upgrade effect types:
 *   auto_builder_count  — number of auto-builders (each places 1 block per interval)
 *   auto_builder_speed  — multiplier on placement speed (per-level)
 *   auto_builder_quality — higher material tiers for auto-placed blocks
 */

import { CONFIG } from '../constants.js';

/** @typedef {import('../state.js').GameState} GameState */
/** @typedef {import('./PhysicsEngine.js').PhysicsEngine} PhysicsEngine */
/** @typedef {import('./EconomyManager.js').EconomyManager} EconomyManager */

export class AutomationManager {

  constructor(physicsEngine, economyManager) {
    this._physics = physicsEngine;
    this._economy = economyManager;
    this._state = null;
    this._cooldown = 0;
    this._nextId = 1000000;
  }

  init(state) {
    this._state = state;
  }

  /**
   * Phase 3: tick auto-builder cooldown.
   */
  update(dt) {
    if (!this._state) return;

    // Get number of auto-builders from upgrades
    const builderCount = this._economy
      ? Math.floor(this._economy.getEffectValue('auto_builder_count'))
      : 0;
    if (builderCount <= 0) {
      this._cooldown = 0; // reset so it fires immediately when upgrade is purchased
      return;
    }

    // Get speed multiplier (higher = faster)
    const speedMult = this._economy
      ? Math.max(0.1, 1 - this._economy.getEffectValue('auto_builder_speed'))
      : 1.0;

    // Base interval: 4s, reduced by speed upgrades
    const interval = Math.max(0.5, CONFIG.AUTO_BUILDER_INTERVAL_S * speedMult);

    this._cooldown -= dt;
    if (this._cooldown > 0) return;

    this._cooldown = interval;

    // Place blocks for each auto-builder
    for (let i = 0; i < builderCount; i++) {
      this._autoPlaceBlock();
    }
  }

  _autoPlaceBlock() {
    const s = this._state;
    const tower = s.tower;
    if (tower.blocks.length >= 500) return; // hard cap

    // Try to place at the tower top center. Offset slightly per builder for variety.
    const materialId = this._economy
      ? Math.min(2, Math.floor(this._economy.getEffectValue('auto_builder_quality')))
      : 0;

    const blockWidth = CONFIG.BLOCK_WIDTH;
    const blockHeight = CONFIG.BLOCK_HEIGHT;

    // Find the top-center position with support
    const topY = -(tower.currentHeight + blockHeight + 2);
    const bx = 0; // center X

    // Check if placement would be valid
    const hasSupport = this._physics.hasSupport(bx, topY, blockWidth, blockHeight);
    const areaFree = this._physics.isAreaFree(bx, topY, blockWidth, blockHeight);
    if (!hasSupport || !areaFree) return;

    // Deduct cost (auto-builders get a 50% discount)
    const cost = { money: Math.floor(CONFIG.BLOCK_BASE_COST * 0.5) };
    if (this._economy && !this._economy.spend(cost)) return;

    const blockId = this._nextId++;
    const newBlock = {
      id: blockId,
      x: bx,
      y: topY,
      width: blockWidth,
      height: blockHeight,
      health: 1.0,
      stress: 0,
      materialId: materialId,
      isWelded: false,
    };

    tower.blocks.push(newBlock);
    this._physics.spawnBlock(newBlock);

    // Update height
    const blockTop = -(topY - blockHeight / 2);
    if (blockTop > tower.currentHeight) tower.currentHeight = blockTop;
    if (tower.currentHeight > tower.maxHeight) tower.maxHeight = tower.currentHeight;

    s.stats.totalBlocksPlaced++;
  }

  serialize() {
    return { nextId: this._nextId, cooldown: this._cooldown };
  }

  deserialize(data, state) {
    this._state = state;
    if (data) {
      this._nextId = data.nextId ?? 1000000;
      this._cooldown = data.cooldown ?? 0;
    }
  }
}

/**
 * DocsModule.js
 * -------------
 * In-game documentation overlay.
 *
 * Fetches docs.html, extracts the content sections (excluding the
 * sidebar and page chrome), and displays them in a scrollable modal
 * overlay within the game.
 *
 * Triggered by a "?" help button in the game UI.
 */

/** @typedef {import('../state.js').GameState} GameState */

export class DocsModule {

  constructor() {
    /** @type {GameState|null} */
    this._state = null;

    /** @type {boolean} */
    this._open = false;

    /** @type {HTMLElement|null} */
    this._overlay = null;
